For hands-free operation just say \"Hey Cortana Control Home\" followed by a command phrase like \"turn on the master bedroom light.\"  Following a successful command, Cortana reads back exactly what your Premise server did, so you know for sure what task was performed.\r\n\r\nThe additional required software Premise Home Control and my Premise SpeechParser module are completely FREE, plus I show step by step videos on how to set everything up on my YouTube channel (see app support link).\r\n\r\nINSTALLATION:\r\nThis app requires that you have a working Premise Home Control server setup already, and it also requires that SpeechPraser be installed on the Premise server.  If you are new to home automation, please see the tutorial videos on my YouTube channel (use app support link) for how to setup the Premise server and the SpeechParser module.\r\n\r\nThis app is meant to be installed on a device other than your Premise server.  This device must be compatible with Windows Universal Apps (e.g. Windows 10 or Windows Phone 8.1 or higher). \r\n\r\nOpen the Cortana Control Home app, and fill in your Premise server address, port, username and password.  Click \"Set Values\" and close the app.  The app itself is just a front end to input the server values.  A background server does all the work by receiving the spoken phrase from Cortana, and then providing Cortana a sentence to read back.\r\n\r\nSince the app uses an HTTP connection, it means sensitive home automation commands will not be encrypted (see warranty section under Additional Terms for more information).\r\n\r\nThis app will send a text string representing what was spoken to your Premise server.
